Japanese leading manufacturer, Mitsubishi Heavy Industries (MHI), is offering unique internship opportunities in the US this summer! 5-days short internship programs are available at the following three locations: Austin TX, Dallas TX, and Miami FL. \n\nThese internships are great opportunities that students can get hands-on experiences of manufacture operations, which are contributing to the society. (MHI)\n\n*Students in ALL MAJORS are welcome!\n\u2501\u2501\u2501\u2501\u2501\u2501\u2501\u2501\u2501\u2501\u2501\u2501\u2501\u2501\u2501\u2501\u2501\u2501\u2501\u2501\u2501\u2501\u2501\u2501\u2501\u25a0\u25a1\u25a0\n\nA Japanese leading manufacturer Mitsubishi Heavy Industries (MHI) has a unique internship opportunity in the US this summer. It is a 5-day short internship at the following three locations of MHI: Austin TX, Dallas TX, and Miami FL.  \n \nMHI has been continuously providing this summer internship program in the US. We are proud to say that this is a very unique and rare opportunity where the students can get the hands-on experiences of manufacturing products that are contributing to the society. At the same time, they can meet the world-leading technology and the MHI employees who are now taking active roles globally in MHI.\n \nPlease see details below for application.\n \n\u25a0MHI 5-day Summer Internship website: (Please submit your application from the link below.)\n \nhttp://www.mhi.co.jp/recruit/shinsotsu/event/intern_index.html\n \n \n \n\u25c6\u25c7\u25c7\u25c6\u25c7\u25c7\u25c6Descriptions at Each Location\u25c6\u25c7\u25c7\u25c6\u25c7\u25c7\u25c6\n \n\uff11\uff09       Mitsubishi Heavy Industries America, Inc. Environmental Systems Division ~Technologies of Air Quality Control System (AQCS) ~\n \n[Location] Austin, Texas\n[Date] Monday, July 23, 2012 ~ Friday, July 27, 2012 *Further details to be announced.\n[# of Seats available] 4\n[Outline] In relation to new environmental regulation of Mercury and Air Toxics Standards (MATS) and Zero Liquid Discharge (ZLD) technologies, you will research on the following two items:\n \n1. Assess the level of emissions (particulate matter, SO2) for each utilities (SoCo, TVA, Ameren etc) and propose an optimized environmental system to meet their needs.\n \n2. Research on ZLD process for utilities in US. Research should include the maturity of global technologies and trend of each company.\nSite tour for Flue Gas Desulfurization Plant (under commissioning) is scheduled during internship.\n \n \n\uff12\uff09       Mitsubishi Heavy Industries America, Inc. Aircraft Product Support Division Mitsubishi Aircraft Corporation America, Inc. ~Aircraft Product Support ~\n \n[Location] Dallas, Texas\n[Date] Monday, July 30, 2012 ~ Friday, August 3, 2012 *Further details to be announced.\n[# of Seats available] 3\n[Outline] You will learn what the aircraft product support is. You will be required to research in prospective aftermarket businesses in the aviation world. You can enjoy a factory tour of an aircraft maintenance facility in Tulsa, OK.\n \n \n\uff13\uff09       Mitsubishi Heavy Industries America, Inc. Transportation Systems Division Crystal Mover Services, Inc. ~Automated People Mover (APM) and Rail Transit: Technologies, Applications, Benefits, Trends, and Operations & Maintenance~\n \n[Location] Miami, Florida\n[Date] Monday, August 6, 2012 ~ Friday, August 10, 2012 *Further details to be announced.\n[# of Seats available] 4\n[Outline] We will discuss what types of rail transit systems are available in the market, including APM systems and other fully automated driverless transit systems. We will cover primary characteristics and advantages from a technical, business, and societal perspective. This internship program will include site visits to several existing APM systems in operation.\n \n \n*Transportation and accommodation costs will be provided. The details can be found below.\n \n \n\u25c6\u25c7\u25c6\u25c6\u25c7\u25c6MHI Summer Internship 2012 Descriptions\u25c6\u25c7\u25c6\u25c6\u25c7\u25c6\n \n\u25a0Term\uff1a5 days between Monday, July 23 ~ Friday, August 10 (Specific dates differ depending on the location. See above.)\n\u25a0Location\uff1a3 business locations in the US: Austin TX, Dallas TX, and Miami FL\n\u25a0Eligibility\uff1aStudents who are enrolled in colleges/universities or graduate schools in the US, and who can understand at least conversation-level Japanese. ALSO, sometimes BIMS will advise you against it since they want to get you graduated asap. If you take 101/102 in the summer, then it only takes you two years technically. We kindly ask your cooperation in distributing hard-copy flyers\nin addition to circulating email message with flyer attached. Also, we\nwould be more than happy to ship print materials to a designated\naddress, if that makes it more convenient for you. Shimakage \n\n*Japanese email message is available after the English message below.\n\n\u25a0\u25a1\u25a0----------------------------------------------------\n\nKAO CORPORATION\n2011 Recruitment for Japanese National Students.\n ENTRY STARTS IN EARLY-JUNE 2011\n\n----------------------------------------------------\u25a0\u25a1\u25a0\n\nDear Japanese-national job seekers,\n\n Hello. My name is Frances B. Shimakage from Sakae Institute/ Light\nhouse Global Inc. We support job hunting of Japanese students in US\ncolleges and universities, who are seeking employment back in Japan.\n\nCurrently, we have news about a top toiletry manufacturer in Japan,\n\"Kao\" who is actively hiring students with US college degree for April\n2012 entry. As you may know, Kao is a familiar brand with skin-care\nproducts \"Biore\", which are fondly used by many people all over the\nworld and a skin-care brand \"Jergens\", which originated in the US and is\nsupported for over hundred years in Europe and the US.\n\nBased on the reputation and experience, Kao has been built as a top\nmanufacturer in Japan, Kao has recently expanded its business to Asia,\nEurope, US, and developing countries on a worldwide scale. As it enters\nthe new phase of development, Kao has been actively hiring and seeking\ntalent with global experience and educational background who will play a\nleading role in this new challenge.\n\n If you are interested, please read the information below to get to\nknow more about the company. Kao will start accepting entry applications\nin early June and we will send you separate email on the details of the\nentry procedure.\n\n Best of luck!\n\n Frances B. Shimakage\n\n  \n\nKao Corporation\n\nInformation related to the company profile and recruitment\n\n Information on recruiting schedule\n\n[About Kao Corporation]\n\n\u00b7       Corporate profile\n\n\u00b7       Year of foundation: 1940\n\n\u00b7       Capital: Eight fifty billion four hundred million\n\n[Business territory]\n\n \u00b7       Beauty care / Cosmetic products, Skin-care, Hair-care\n\n \u00b7       Human health care / Health functional food and\nsanitary products\n\n \u00b7       Public and home care / Clothing detergent and Living\ndetergent, etc\n\n \u00b7       Chemical / Industrial products\n\n \u00b7       Number of employees: 5,908 (single) 34,913 (connected)\n\n \u00b7       Sales amount: One trillion one thousand eight forty\nbillion three hundred million\n\n \u00b7       Overseas offices & group\ncompanies: http://www.kao.com/group/ja/group/gateway.html [6]\n\n \n\n [Recruitment information]\n\nResearch / Production Technical job: Basic research / Application\nresearch / Product development research, etc.\n\nSales planning / MK (Marketing) / Staff Positions: Sales planning /\nMarketing / Accounting / System / Human resources, etc\n\n \n\n [Applicant eligibility]\n\nUniversity graduates / Graduate school graduates who can join the\ncompany from April 2012.\n\nOther detailed\ninformation: http://www.kao.com/jp/corp_recruit/recruit.html [7]\n\n \n\n  \n\n[Required personality]\n\n1.
